    <h2 class="sow-headline"><a href="https://www.openproject.org/collaboration-software-features/#product-management" title="Product management and roadmap planning">Product management and roadmap planning</a></h2></div></div></div><div id="panel-w5937f5ce7270e-0-1-1" class="so-panel widget widget_sow-editor panel-last-child" data-index="2" ><div class="so-widget-sow-editor so-widget-sow-editor-base">
<div class="siteorigin-widget-tinymce textwidget">
	<p>OpenProject is the easiest way to plan and communicate your product roadmap and break it down into a detailed release plan.</p>
<p><a class="readmore" title="Learn more about product management and roadmap planning" href="https://www.openproject.org/collaboration-software-features/#product-management">Learn more</a></p>
</div>
</div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div id="pgc-w5937f6342c46c-0-1"  class="panel-grid-cell" ><div id="panel-w5937f6342c46c-0-1-0" class="so-panel widget widget_siteorigin-panels-builder panel-first-child panel-last-child" data-index="1" ><div class="landingpage-row__blue-features-item panel-widget-style panel-widget-style-for-w5937f6342c46c-0-1-0" ><div id="pl-w5937f6342c4e6"  class="panel-layout" ><div id="pg-w5937f6342c4e6-0"  class="panel-grid panel-no-style" ><div id="pgc-w5937f6342c4e6-0-0"  class="panel-grid-cell" ><div id="panel-w5937f6342c4e6-0-0-0" class="so-panel widget widget_sow-image panel-first-child panel-last-child" data-index="0" ><div class="so-widget-sow-image so-widget-sow-image-default-eef982a7180b">

<div class="sow-image-container">
<a href="https://www.openproject.org/collaboration-software-features/#agile-scrum" >	<img src="https://1t1rycb9er64f1pgy2iuseow-wpengine.netdna-ssl.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/11/feature-agile-and-scrum-white-01.png" width="192" height="134" sizes="(max-width: 192px) 100vw, 192px" title="Agile &amp; Scrum" alt="Agile &amp; Scrum" 		class="so-widget-image"/>

</div></div></div><div id="pgc-w5937f6342c4e6-0-1"  class="panel-grid-cell" ><div id="panel-w5937f6342c4e6-0-1-0" class="so-panel widget widget_sow-headline panel-first-child" data-index="1" ><div class="so-widget-sow-headline so-widget-sow-headline-default-729d08827087"><div class="sow-headline-container ">
    <h2 class="sow-headline"><a href="https://www.openproject.org/collaboration-software-features/#agile-scrum" title="Agile and Scrum">Agile &amp; Scrum</a></h2></div></div></div><div id="panel-w5937f6342c4e6-0-1-1" class="so-panel widget widget_sow-editor panel-last-child" data-index="2" ><div class="so-widget-sow-editor so-widget-sow-editor-base">
<div class="siteorigin-widget-tinymce textwidget">
	<p>High performance teams iterate fast and release constantly. OpenProject provides the perfect tool to support agile product development<br />
methodologies such as Scrum and Kanban.</p>
<p><a class="readmore" title="Learn more about agile and scrum" href="https://www.openproject.org/collaboration-software-features/#agile-scrum">Learn more</a></p>
</div>

    <h2 class="sow-headline"><a href="https://www.openproject.org/collaboration-software-features/#bug-tracking" title="Bug tracking">Bug tracking</a></h2></div></div></div><div id="panel-w5937f7be30427-0-1-1" class="so-panel widget widget_sow-editor panel-last-child" data-index="2" ><div class="so-widget-sow-editor so-widget-sow-editor-base">
<div class="siteorigin-widget-tinymce textwidget">
	<p>OpenProject allows your team to easily track, prioritize and fix bugs. It is the most intuitive and flexible open source bug tracking tool.</p>

    <h2 class="sow-headline"><a href="https://www.openproject.org/collaboration-software-features/#time-tracking" title="Time tracking, cost reporting and budgeting">Time tracking, cost reporting and budgeting</a></h2></div></div></div><div id="panel-w5937f7be3366f-0-1-1" class="so-panel widget widget_sow-editor panel-last-child" data-index="2" ><div class="so-widget-sow-editor so-widget-sow-editor-base">

    <h2 class="sow-headline">OpenProject Enterprise Edition</h2><p class="sow-sub-headline">OpenProject Enterprise Edition builds on top of the Community Edition and includes extra<br /> features mainly aimed at organizations with more than 50 users that manage business critical<br /> projects with OpenProject </p></div></div></div></div></div><div id="pg-w5937f885ba2b8-1"  class="panel-grid panel-has-style" ><div class="panel-row-style panel-row-style-for-w5937f885ba2b8-1" ><div id="pgc-w5937f885ba2b8-1-0"  class="panel-grid-cell" ><div id="panel-w5937f885ba2b8-1-0-0" class="so-panel widget widget_sow-image panel-first-child" data-index="1" ><div class="so-widget-sow-image so-widget-sow-image-default-eef982a7180b">

<div class="sow-image-container">
<a href="https://openproject.org/download-and-installation" >	<img src="https://1t1rycb9er64f1pgy2iuseow-wpengine.netdna-ssl.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/openproject-community-edition-icon.png" width="480" height="373" srcset="/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/openproject-community-edition-icon.png 480w, /wp-content/uploads/2016/10/openproject-community-edition-icon-300x233.png 300w, /wp-content/uploads/2016/10/openproject-community-edition-icon-250x194.png 250w" sizes="(max-width: 480px) 100vw, 480px" title="Community Edition" alt="Community Edition" 		class="so-widget-image"/>
</a></div>

</div></div><div id="panel-w5937f885ba2b8-1-0-1" class="so-panel widget widget_sow-headline" data-index="2" ><div class="so-widget-sow-headline so-widget-sow-headline-default-561cf9d08ebb"><div class="sow-headline-container ">
    <h3 class="sow-headline"><a href="https://openproject.org/download-and-installation/" title="Community Edition">Community Edition</a></h3></div></div></div><div id="panel-w5937f885ba2b8-1-0-2" class="so-panel widget widget_sow-editor panel-last-child" data-index="3" ><div class="so-widget-sow-editor so-widget-sow-editor-base">
<div class="siteorigin-widget-tinymce textwidget">
	<p style="text-align: center;">The OpenProject Community edition is the leading open source project management software that comes with regular updates and new releases for free.</p>
</div>
</div></div></div><div id="pgc-w5937f885ba2b8-1-1"  class="panel-grid-cell" ><div id="panel-w5937f885ba2b8-1-1-0" class="so-panel widget widget_sow-editor panel-first-child panel-last-child" data-index="4" ><div class="circle-vs panel-widget-style panel-widget-style-for-w5937f885ba2b8-1-1-0" ><div class="so-widget-sow-editor so-widget-sow-editor-base">
<div class="siteorigin-widget-tinymce textwidget">
	<p>vs</p>
</div>
</div></div></div></div><div id="pgc-w5937f885ba2b8-1-2"  class="panel-grid-cell" ><div id="panel-w5937f885ba2b8-1-2-0" class="so-panel widget widget_sow-image panel-first-child" data-index="5" ><div class="so-widget-sow-image so-widget-sow-image-default-eef982a7180b">
